          </ul>
        </nav>

  <section class="l-content-width section section--bordered">
    <div class="section__description">
      <h2 class="section__headline visuallyhidden">Descripción</h2>
      <div class="l-row">
          <div class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  l-column small-12 medium-9 large-8" dir>
        

        <p dir="false" data-test-bidi>Getting lazy looking for the remote control hiding somewhere in the house. We have the solution Remote TV Controller allows you to remotely control your TV set using your iPhone/iPad or simply using your brand new Apple Watch.<br /><br />The app has been crafted and designed with most ergonomic elements and is the first app that helps you control your TV simply using your Apple Watch<br /><br />The app supports all the Smart TVs since 2015 including the latest N Series (2018).<br /><br />The main features are:<br /><br />[+] Compatibility with the majority of Smart TVs<br /><br />[+] Turn ON and OFF the TV<br /><br />[+] Change channels.<br /><br />[+] Increase or decrease the volume (also using the iPhone side buttons and the crown on the Apple Watch)<br /><br />[+] Mute the sound (silent mode)<br /><br />[+] Change the source (HDMI, PC, AV ... etc.)<br /><br />[+] Access the Smart TV area<br /><br />[+] Access the 4 favorite buttons<br /><br />[+] Enter channel numbers using the numeric keypad<br /><br />[+] Quickly launch Netflix and other apps<br /><br />[+] Siri Shortcuts to quickly interact with your TV using only your voice<br /><br />We have integrated the most useful command that we usually use in everyday life. <br /><br />More command will be added in future releases.<br /><br />Please leave us a review if you like the app and your feedbacks are welcome.<br /><br />Enjoy<br /><br />Disclaimer:<br />This app is not an official Samsung application. We are not affiliated with Samsung Electronics in any way.<br /><br />Privacy policy: https://quanticapps.com/remote-tv/privacy<br />Terms of use: https://quanticapps.com/remote-tv/terms</p>
    


<!----></div>


      </div>
    </div>

    <h3 class="we-truncate we-truncate--single-line  we-customer-review__title" dir="ltr" id="we-customer-review-48689">
    Exvelente. Falta elegir que appl. queremos y cuales no.
</h3>



      <blockquote class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  we-customer-review__body" dir>
        

        <p dir="false" data-test-bidi>Seria genial poder controlar otros dispositivos como Apple TV , Receptores Onkio , etc... <br /><br />-El trackpad no funciona en las aplicaciones. <br /><br />-Se debería poder elegir que aplicaciones queremos tener y poder borrar las que no usamos.</p>
